files in apache/kafka implementing Kafka Streams DSL operations and their corresponding Processor API equivalents to support migration from DSL to the lower-level Processor API.\\n\\n## Key Findings\\n\\n### DSL Interfaces and Implementations\\n\\nThe Kafka Streams DSL is defined through interfaces in the `kstream` package:\\n- **KStream.java**: Defines DSL operations including `filter()`, `filterNot()`, `map()`, `mapValues()`, `flatMap()`, `flatMapValues()`, `selectKey()`, `groupByKey()`, and `groupBy()` methods.\\n- **KTable.java**: Similar operations for stateful tables including `filter()`, `filterNot()`, `mapValues()`, and `groupBy()`.\\n- **KGroupedStream.java** and **KGroupedTable.java**: Represent grouped streams and tables for aggregation operations.\\n\\nThe implementations are in the `internals` subpackage:\\n- **KStreamImpl.java**: Implements all KStream DSL operations. Each operation (e.g., `filter()`, `map()`, `mapValues()`, `groupBy()`) creates a `ProcessorGraphNode` wrapping a `ProcessorSupplier` that uses the Processor API underneath.\\n- **KTableImpl.java**: Similar implementation for KTable operations.\\n- **KGroupedStreamImpl.java** and **KGroupedTableImpl.java**: Handle grouped stream/table operations.\\n\\n### DSL-to-Processor API Mapping\\n\\nThe migration pathway from DSL to Processor API is clearly demonstrated through ProcessorSupplier implementations:\\n\\n**Filter Operations:**\\n- DSL: `KStream.filter(Predicate)` → Implementation: `KStreamImpl.filter()` → Processor: `KStreamFilter` implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>` containing `KStreamFilterProcessor` extends `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor<K, V, V>`\\n- DSL: `KTable.filter(Predicate)` → Implementation: `KTableImpl.filter()` → Processor: `KTableFilter`\\n\\n**Map Operations:**\\n- DSL: `KStream.map(KeyValueMapper)` → Implementation: `KStreamImpl.map()` → Processor: `KStreamMap` implements `ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>` containing `KStreamMapProcessor` extends `ContextualProcessor<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>`\\n- DSL: `KStream.mapValues(ValueMapper)` → Implementation: `KStreamImpl.mapValues()` → Processor: `KStreamMapValues` implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, VOut>`\\n- DSL: `KStream.flatMap(KeyValueMapper)` → Implementation: `KStreamImpl.flatMap()` → Processor: `KStreamFlatMap` implements `ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>`\\n- DSL: `KStream.flatMapValues(ValueMapper)` → Implementation: `KStreamImpl.flatMapValues()` → Processor: `KStreamFlatMapValues`\\n- DSL: `KTable.mapValues(ValueMapper)` → Implementation: `KTableImpl.mapValues()` → Processor: `KTableMapValues`\\n\\n**Group Operations:**\\n- DSL: `KStream.groupBy(KeyValueMapper)` and `KStream.groupByKey()` → Implementation: `KStreamImpl.groupBy()` and `KStreamImpl.groupByKey()` → Processor: Uses `KStreamMap` internally via `internalSelectKey()` followed by `KGroupedStreamImpl` creation\\n\\n### Processor API Foundation\\n\\nThe Processor API provides the low-level abstractions:\\n- **Processor.java** and **FixedKeyProcessor.java**: Core processor interfaces that implement the actual record processing logic.\\n- **ProcessorSupplier.java** and **FixedKeyProcessorSupplier.java**: Factory interfaces for creating processor instances.\\n- **ContextualProcessor.java** and **ContextualFixedKeyProcessor.java**: Base classes providing access to `ProcessorContext`.\\n- **Record.java** and **FixedKeyRecord.java**: Record abstractions for the Processor API.\\n- **ProcessorContext.java** and **FixedKeyProcessorContext.java**: Context for state store access and output forwarding.\\n\\n### Graph Integration\\n\\nThe topology graph structures the operations:\\n- **ProcessorGraphNode.java**: Represents a processor node in the topology graph.\\n- **ProcessorParameters.java**: Encapsulates the processor supplier and processor name.\\n- **GraphNode.java**: Base abstraction for topology graph nodes.\\n\\n### Supporting Infrastructure\\n\\nFunctional interfaces and configuration classes:\\n- **Predicate.java**: Used by filter operations\\n- **KeyValueMapper.java**: Used by map/flatMap operations\\n- **ValueMapper.java** and **ValueMapperWithKey.java**: Used by mapValues/flatMapValues operations\\n- **Grouped.java** and **GroupedInternal.java**: Configuration for grouping operations\\n- **GroupedStreamAggregateBuilder.java**: Builds aggregations on grouped streams\\n\\n### Aggregation Support\\n\\nFor teams migrating groupBy operations to the Processor API with custom state stores:\\n- **KStreamAggregate.java**: DSL aggregation processor\\n- **KStreamReduce.java**, **KTableReduce.java**: Reduction operations\\n- **KStreamWindowAggregate.java**, **KStreamSessionWindowAggregate.java**, **KStreamSlidingWindowAggregate.java**: Windowed aggregation processors\\n- **KStreamAggProcessorSupplier.java**: ProcessorSupplier for aggregations\\n\\nThis architecture shows that teams can migrate from DSL by directly using the ProcessorSupplier implementations (KStreamFilter, KStreamMap, KStreamMapValues, etc.) or by implementing custom `ProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` classes for operations needing custom state management, then adding them to the topology via the Processor `filter()`, `filterNot()`, `map()`, `mapValues()`, `flatMap()`, `flatMapValues()`, `selectKey()`, `groupByKey()`, and `groupBy()` methods.\\n- **KTable.java**: Similar operations for stateful tables including `filter()`, `filterNot()`, `mapValues()`, and `groupBy()`.\\n- **KGroupedStream.java** and **KGroupedTable.java**: Represent grouped streams and tables for aggregation operations.\\n\\nThe implementations are in the `internals` subpackage:\\n- **KStreamImpl.java**: Implements all KStream DSL operations. Each operation (e.g., `filter()`, `map()`, `mapValues()`, `groupBy()`) creates a `ProcessorGraphNode` wrapping a `ProcessorSupplier` that uses the Processor API underneath.\\n- **KTableImpl.java**: Similar implementation for KTable operations.\\n- **KGroupedStreamImpl.java** and **KGroupedTableImpl.java**: Handle grouped stream/table operations.\\n\\n### DSL-to-Processor API Mapping\\n\\nThe migration pathway from DSL to Processor API is clearly demonstrated through ProcessorSupplier implementations:\\n\\n**Filter Operations:**\\n- DSL: `KStream.filter(Predicate)` → Implementation: `KStreamImpl.filter()` → Processor: `KStreamFilter` implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>` containing `KStreamFilterProcessor` extends `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor<K, V, V>`\\n- DSL: `KTable.filter(Predicate)` → Implementation: `KTableImpl.filter()` → Processor: `KTableFilter`\\n\\n**Map Operations:**\\n- DSL: `KStream.map(KeyValueMapper)` → Implementation: `KStreamImpl.map()` → Processor: `KStreamMap` implements `ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>` containing `KStreamMapProcessor` extends `ContextualProcessor<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>`\\n- DSL: `KStream.mapValues(ValueMapper)` → Implementation: `KStreamImpl.mapValues()` → Processor: `KStreamMapValues` implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, VOut>`\\n- DSL: `KStream.flatMap(KeyValueMapper)` → Implementation: `KStreamImpl.flatMap()` → Processor: `KStreamFlatMap` implements `ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>`\\n- DSL: `KStream.flatMapValues(ValueMapper)` → Implementation: `KStreamImpl.flatMapValues()` → Processor: `KStreamFlatMapValues`\\n- DSL: `KTable.mapValues(ValueMapper)` → Implementation: `KTableImpl.mapValues()` → Processor: `KTableMapValues`\\n\\n**Group Operations:**\\n- DSL: `KStream.groupBy(KeyValueMapper)` and `KStream.groupByKey()` → Implementation: `KStreamImpl.groupBy()` and `KStreamImpl.groupByKey()` → Processor: Uses `KStreamMap` internally via `internalSelectKey()` followed by `KGroupedStreamImpl` creation\\n\\n### Processor API Foundation\\n\\nThe Processor API provides the low-level abstractions:\\n- **Processor.java** and **FixedKeyProcessor.java**: Core processor interfaces that implement the actual record processing logic.\\n- **ProcessorSupplier.java** and **FixedKeyProcessorSupplier.java**: Factory interfaces for creating processor instances.\\n- **ContextualProcessor.java** and **ContextualFixedKeyProcessor.java**: Base classes providing access to `ProcessorContext`.\\n- **Record.java** and **FixedKeyRecord.java**: Record abstractions for the Processor API.\\n- **ProcessorContext.java** and **FixedKeyProcessorContext.java**: Context for state store access and output forwarding.\\n\\n### Graph Integration\\n\\nThe topology graph structures the operations:\\n- **ProcessorGraphNode.java**: Represents a processor node in the topology graph.\\n- **ProcessorParameters.java**: Encapsulates the processor supplier and processor name.\\n- **GraphNode.java**: Base abstraction for topology graph nodes.\\n\\n### Supporting Infrastructure\\n\\nFunctional interfaces and configuration classes:\\n- **Predicate.java**: Used by filter operations\\n- **KeyValueMapper.java**: Used by map/flatMap operations\\n- **ValueMapper.java** and **ValueMapperWithKey.java**: Used by mapValues/flatMapValues operations\\n- **Grouped.java** and **GroupedInternal.java**: Configuration for grouping operations\\n- **GroupedStreamAggregateBuilder.java**: Builds aggregations on grouped streams\\n\\n### Aggregation Support\\n\\nFor teams migrating groupBy operations to the Processor API with custom state stores:\\n- **KStreamAggregate.java**: DSL aggregation processor\\n- **KStreamReduce.java**, **KTableReduce.java**: Reduction operations\\n- **KStreamWindowAggregate.java**, **KStreamSessionWindowAggregate.java**, **KStreamSlidingWindowAggregate.java**: Windowed aggregation processors\\n- **KStreamAggProcessorSupplier.java**: ProcessorSupplier for aggregations\\n\\nThis architecture shows that teams can migrate from DSL by directly using the ProcessorSupplier implementations (KStreamFilter, KStreamMap, KStreamMapValues, etc.) or by implementing custom `ProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` classes for operations needing custom state management, then adding them to the topology via the Processor API.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
